<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_389c6e53-8244-4443-9e78-4bc368b41e2e'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

  <span id="freeText1263227748738458187" style="display:none">Nineteen-year-old Cheyenne tries to portray the perfect life to mask the memories of her past. Walking in on her boyfriend with another woman her freshman year in college threatens that picture of perfection. <br /><br />Twenty-one-year-old Colt never wanted college and never expected to amount to anything, but when his mom's dying wish is for him to get his degree, he has no choice but to pretend it's what he wants too. <br /><br />Cheyenne needs a fake boyfriend to get back at her ex and Colt needs cash to take care of his mom, so they strike a deal that helps them both. But what if Cheyenne’s past isn’t what she thought? Soon they’re trading one charade for another—losing themselves in each other to forget about their pain. The more they play their game, the more it becomes the only thing they have that feels real.<br /><br />Both Cheyenne and Colt know life is never easy, but neither of them expect the tragedy that threatens to end their charade and rip them apart forever.</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer502217790" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer5758666324835416076"><br/>Hello Readers!!<br/><br/>Her life's perfect.<br/><br/>She's Cheyenne Marshall.She was the captain of the dance team.Voted most popular girl in her high school.She had friends.Tons of them.<br/><br/>But here in college she knows everyone through her perfect boyfriend Gregory.<br/><br/>But then...she finds Gregory cheating on her with someone else.<br/><br/><b>

</b></span>
  <span id="freeText5758666324835416076" style="display:none"><br />Hello Readers!!<br /><br />Her life's perfect.<br /><br />She's Cheyenne Marshall.She was the captain of the dance team.Voted most popular girl in her high school.She had friends.Tons of them.<br /><br />But here in college she knows everyone through her perfect boyfriend Gregory.<br /><br />But then...she finds Gregory cheating on her with someone else.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>'What is it about me that makes people think they can take advantage and toss me aside?Why am I so easy to betray?'</i>
</b><br /><br />No,not everything is as it seems.<br /><br />So,her seemingly perfect life is a.....<b>
  <i>CHARADE!!</i>
</b><br /><br />A charade she has always played to perfection.<br /><br /><b>All her life she has hidden behind a mask no one can see.<br /><br />The mask of a perfect person with a perfect life.</b><br /><br /><i>Now no one can just toss aside and leave a perfect person.Can they??</i><br /><br /><br /><br />His life is as far from perfect as you can get.<br /><br />Colt's mom is dying.And she wants him to be better than what his legacy is.She wants him to get a degree.<br /><br />So,he's in college getting a degree for his mom.<br /><br />Tall,messy blonde hair and skin covered with ink,he's hot.<br /><br />But he's also an asshole,to be very precise!!<br /><br />Also,he's the only guy who Gregory is afraid to cross.<br /><br /><br /><b>So,the two of them decide to play a new charade together.</b><br /><br />Chey wants to show Gregory and others that her life is still absolutely perfect.So seeing the animosity between Colt and Gregory,she asks Colt to pose as her boyfriend to make Gregory jealous.In return she will pay him.<br /><br />Colt needs money anyhow,for his mom.He agrees.<br /><br /><br /><i>And thus begins the greatest charade of their lives....</i><br /><br /><br /><br />Charade.It's all a charade.<br /><br />Then why can't she hide from him? Why only he can see the real her?<br /><br />Why,when she has never needed anyone,does she ask him to keep her safe?<br /><br /><b>
  <i>'Him being here is like he's picking at the edge of a sticker.Using his nail to peel back a layer of me that I can't handle removing.'</i>
</b><br /><br /><br />Charade.It's all a charade.<br /><br /><br />Then why does he give a damn? Why is he intent upon baring the real her?<br /><br />Why,when he doesn't give a damn about anyone else except his mother,is he doing everything to make her feel safe and happy?And most importantly,why does he want to change?<br /><br /><b>
  <i>'I'm tired.So fucking tired of fighting it and feeling this way--whatever the hell way it is.I lie about everything.I'm a dick to everyone.I can't even truthfully answer the question "are you happy".But she sees more in me.'</i>
</b><br /><br /><br />And suddenly they find that this little charade of theirs,is more real than anything else.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"I thought this was a game."<br /><br />"Not anymore and you know it.Everything else in my life is all fucked up.This is the only thing that's real."</i>
</b><br /><br /><br /><i>But is this???</i><br /><br /><br />After they have been playing for so long,they will now have to prove that what they have is real.<br /><br />Specially in the face of an impending tragedy.<br /><br /><i>Will they be able to do so???</i><br /><br />Well you have to read this to find out.<br /><br /><br /><b>That's all for now,Readers.<br /><br />Ta-Ta!!</b><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="5758666324835416076" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_448321382" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/448321382" />
    <a title="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8524618-angie---angie-s-dreamy-reads"><img alt="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1578074503p2/8524618.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/448321382?book_show_action=true">Nov 04, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" href="/user/show/8524618-angie---angie-s-dreamy-reads">Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer448321382" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10309444485085886032"><b>4.5 HEART WARMING STARS</b><br/><br/><br/><b>HEART ACHE<br/>ANGER<br/>REVENGE<br/>LIFE<br/>LOVE<br/>DEATH<br/>GRIEVING<br/>HEALING<br/>MOVING ON<br/>LIVING<br/>HAPPINESS<br/>E.M.O.T.I.O.N.A.L</b><br/><br/><i>This book covers everything that can happen to you that I would consider <u>'tragic'</u> but it's also a message of a love that can heal and can help you learn to move on, to emerge stronger. To not carry all of life's up's and downs on your shoulders but to let someone you LOVE shoulder those burdens with you. Let them carry you through those tough days. Love can be healing. Love is amazin</i></span>
  <span id="freeText10309444485085886032" style="display:none"><b>4.5 HEART WARMING STARS</b><br><br><br><b>HEART ACHE<br>ANGER<br>REVENGE<br>LIFE<br>LOVE<br>DEATH<br>GRIEVING<br>HEALING<br>MOVING ON<br>LIVING<br>HAPPINESS<br>E.M.O.T.I.O.N.A.L</b><br><br><i>This book covers everything that can happen to you that I would consider <u>'tragic'</u> but it's also a message of a love that can heal and can help you learn to move on, to emerge stronger. To not carry all of life's up's and downs on your shoulders but to let someone you LOVE shoulder those burdens with you. Let them carry you through those tough days. Love can be healing. Love is amazing. Love can make a broken heart whole again!! </i><br><br><br><b>WOW</b> this was an amazing surprise. I was paging through my Kindle trying to figure out what I wanted to read when I landed on it and thought <i>"hmmmm...let me read a couple pages and see what I think,"!!!!</i> Well, <b>I.COULD.NOT.PUT.IT.DOWN!!!!!!</b> This is the first Nyrae Dawn book I have read and most certainly will not be my last. I was an emotional wreck while reading it. I don't know what I was expecting, maybe another fluffy romance type book which it most definitely was not. I think this book falls in to the New Adult category which I'm really coming to love. It was heartbreaking to see these two young people struggle with tragedy's that would cripple even a full grown adult. It was beautifully written and the ENDING was OH.MY.GOD intense. It was a full reading experience. I loved every second.<br><br><br><b>
  <i>"This is a game. Our game. One that I asked for, but with each day it feels more real. More real than anything ever has and I'm not sure how I feel about that. What to do. I shouldn't fall for this guy. He's got so much on his plate and he's not the kind of guy to really fall for someone. ~~ Chey</i>
</b><br><br><br>Cheyenne is two weeks into College her freshmen year when she walks in on her Boyfriend of two years with another girl. Upset and angry Chey decides she's going to teach Gregory a lesson and let him know that she doesn't really need him anymore. She's intent on keeping up an image that she has everything in her life going perfectly. She see's Colt in a coffee shop after he's had a confrontation with Gregory and decides he's the perfect guy to teach her ex a lesson. After striking a deal with Colt they begin a charade to make her ex jealous. It's not one sided though Colt get's something out of this to. His mother is dying of cancer and Colt is struggling to pay for things. He needs extra money to be able to afford some additional bills that are coming up in the future. So together they begin a mutually beneficial relationship but little do they know, they're going to be getting a lot more than they signed up for. <br><br><br>Cheyenne has some deep personal issues. Her mother abandoned her when she was younger. She dropped her off at her aunt's house and never came back. Her mother had a habit of deserting her though and an episode that she experienced when she was younger leaves her scarred and with reoccurring panic attacks and nightmares. Cheyenne learned at a young age to never depend on anyone but her break up with Gregory leaves her vulnerable and on edge.<br><br>Colt's a little rough around the edges. He's a bad boy with tattoo's and a dirty mouth. He's struggling with the fact his mom is dying from Cancer and to mask the pain that causes, he's an asshole to everyone around him. It's just a facade though, he's really the sweetest, kindest person. I adored him, cried over him and wanted to hug him. My heart broke for him. One part in this book had me clutching my chest. His pain is palpable. It's really intense. <br><br><b>
  <i>"I thought this was a game," I reminded him.<br>"Not anymore and you know it. Everything else in my life is all f*cked up. This is the only thing that's real." ~~ Colt</i>
</b><br><br><br>Together Chey and Colt find a safe place in each other. A place they can go to, to forget about their problems and their struggles. It starts out as a charade but quickly develops into an escape and then something so much deeper. It's beautiful to read. I loved that at the worst times in their lives they were able to find something as sweet and incredible as love in each other. <br><br><b>
  <i>"This girl is mine. I've had quite a few girls before, but none of them were mine. I didn't want them a part of me, to keep them, and with her I want nothing more that to keep her safe and keep her with me all the time."</i>
</b><br><br>Overall...I thought this book was fantastic. The writing was incredible. I wanted and craved the characters. I was sad when it came to an end. I think Colt and Chey are perfect for each other and the epilogue left me feeling amazing. I can't wait for the second installment in this series. This is an absolute <b>MUST READ.</b><br><br><br><br><u>I Thought this little poem fit Colt and Chey perfectly.</u> <br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396482i/764292.jpg" width="360" height="248" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><u>
  <b> I saw this and it made me think of Colt 3 </b>
</u><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379799521i/655936._SY540_.jpg" width="500" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="10309444485085886032" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="&quot;That&#39;s All&quot; Ash" class="user" itemprop="url" name="&quot;That&#39;s All&quot; Ash" href="/user/show/5606933-that-s-all-ash">&quot;That&#39;s All&quot; Ash</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer559864226" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7672573783329847008"><a href='http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/Vo9EC.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413204i/813271.jpg' alt=' photo Vo9EC.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><a href='http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/download-20.png.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413204i/813272.png' alt=' photo download-20.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>This book <i>literally</i> starts out with a *<b>bang</b>* as college freshman, Cheyenne, catches her boyfriend in bed with another girl. Betrayal isn’t even in the same ballpark for what Cheyenne feels when she walks in on “the guy she was supposed to live happily ever after with” getting it on with someone else.<br/><br/>No no no no no no no no no <b>NO!</b> <br/><br/>This wasn’t supposed to happen to her: the girl voted “Most Popular” in high school; captain of her dance squad; the girl with a million friends. She had writte</span>
  <span id="freeText7672573783329847008" style="display:none"><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/Vo9EC.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413204i/813271.jpg" alt=" photo Vo9EC.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/download-20.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413204i/813272.png" alt=" photo download-20.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This book <i>literally</i> starts out with a *<b>bang</b>* as college freshman, Cheyenne, catches her boyfriend in bed with another girl. Betrayal isn’t even in the same ballpark for what Cheyenne feels when she walks in on “the guy she was supposed to live happily ever after with” getting it on with someone else.<br><br>No no no no no no no no no <b>NO!</b> <br><br>This wasn’t supposed to happen to her: the girl voted “Most Popular” in high school; captain of her dance squad; the girl with a million friends. She had written the perfect life for herself and getting cheated on wasn’t in the script!<br><br>Of course, the cheating jerk tries to manipulate the situation by telling Cheyenne that “he just missed her too much and what was a guy to do?” But she won’t have any of it, as she’s determined to live life as the strong girl she made herself become.<br><br>So she does the smart thing, walks away, and completely removes him from her life.<br><br><b>But not until she tells her good ol’ cheating ex that she cheated on him first</b>. Which is a big, fat, massive, obese lie. But what’s a girl supposed to do, right? Hell hath no fury like a girl who just caught her boyfriend in bed with a buxom red-head and all that jazz. ;)<br><br>So now all Cheyenne has to do is find a guy to pretend to be her boyfriend for a little bit. It’s just a simple problem that just needs a simple answer.<br><br>Too bad she finds probably the most complex guy on campus to act as her simple solution.<br><br>Enter: Colt. A mega badass badboy with dark blonde hair, an upper body rippled with tattoos, and bedsheets that should probably be washed on a daily basis. (I’m not going to lie to you, Colt gave me hot flashes. Aaaaaaaand I’m only twenty-three.)<br><br>So when Cheyenne sees Colt nearly come to blows with her ex in the middle of a coffee house, she knows she’s found a guy who hates the egotistical slime ball as much as she does.<br><br><b>Bingo.</b><br><br>Too bad he turns her down faster than she can even introduce herself.<br><br><i>
  <b>“Forget it,” Colt says. “Good luck, Princess.”<br><br>He’s walking away. My one chance to save face is walking away, and I can feel myself clinging, needing something, anything.<br><br>“I’ll pay you!” I say to his back.<br><br>“Wrong answer. I don’t need your money.”<br><br>And with that, he walks away.</b>
</i><br><br>But don’t worry, friends. This is all the beginning. If that was all to the story, we’d have a very short book on our hands, wouldn’t we? Besides… remember when I told you that Colt is a very sexy and complicated guy?<br><br>Well he’s also a very <b>broke</b> sexy and complicated guy. And he desperately needs money for <b>something</b>. So what does he do? He finds the very sexy, but annoyingly high maintenance girl who proposed a ludicrous idea to him.<br><br>And then he pretends to be her boyfriend.<br><br>I absolutely loved these two characters when they were together! They had such a thick wire of sexual tension between the two, and what I <b>really</b> loved was that they desperately didn’t want it to be there. The didn’t <b>want</b> to share this super strong attraction, but at the same time… they couldn’t stop it.<br><br><i>
  <b>”Neandertals have better mouths than you do.”<br><br>“I think you’d like my mouth, Princess.”<br><br>She gasps and I suddenly want to make good on my threat. I want to suck the lobe of her ear into my mouth. Kiss the spot behind it to see if it drives her wild.</b>
</i><br><br>I also loved when they weren’t around people and it was just the two of them… not only did they stop pretending; they started becoming real. <b>Real</b> people with excruciatingly <b>real</b> problems covered in real secrets.<br><br>While pretending to be lovers and driving Cheyenne’s ex absolutely crazy… they became friends in a sense. True, they still couldn’t decide whether they wanted to kiss or kill one another… but they began to see that the other wasn’t quite who they thought they were. Cheyenne begins to see why Colt has such a hardened exterior. And Colt starts to understand why Cheyenne wants to be so perfect all the time. <br><br><i>
  <b>I feel her shaking as she cries, but no sounds come out. She’s locked up so tight and I both respect her for protecting herself and want to set her free at the same time.” </b>
</i><br><br>And soon what began as a charade turns into something else entirely. As hard as they fight the attraction between them, it keeps building and building until it becomes a wildfire that helps them shed light on the darkness they hold inside.<br><br><br><i>
  <b> I hold her while she sleeps. I don’t know how in the fuck we got here, but somehow this game is more real than anything else.<br><br>And I want it.<br><br>I fucking want it. </b>
</i><br><br>As this book dwindled down towards its ending, I’m not going to lie: I had NO IDEA how big and consuming that darkness was! Holy frijoles, dude! I wasn’t expecting that! But I think that’s what really drove this book home for me. Because things got way intense!<br><br>Well played, Nyrae Dawn…<br><br>Well played. ;)<br><br>4 stars.<br><br><b>CASTING</b><br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/8819b49053b51e9d7e8868b9aea0460a.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413204i/813273.jpg" alt=" photo 8819b49053b51e9d7e8868b9aea0460a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/b6f85835900f1d5ca8f3df3e08a75ad5.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413204i/813274.jpg" alt=" photo b6f85835900f1d5ca8f3df3e08a75ad5.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/download-21.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413204i/813275.jpg" alt=" photo download-21.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/131ac8a77b950a3d6ba69330d42d6027.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413204i/813276._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 131ac8a77b950a3d6ba69330d42d6027.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/15993374.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413204i/813277._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 15993374.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>

<div id="review_443050298" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/443050298" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/443050298?book_show_action=true">Oct 27, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer443050298" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18322258142131746528"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395684i/762112._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i> <b> "This is a game. Our game. One that I asked for, but with each day it feels more real. More real than anything every has.... What to do. I shouldn't fall for this guy." </b></i> <br/><br/>When Cheyenne's heart is broken after finding her boyfriend in bed with another girl, she wants to find a way to make it clear to him that she doesn't need him in her life. Colt is struggling with pushing himself though school to keep a promise he made to his dying mother. When Cheyenne sees him in a coffee shop, she proposes </span>
  <span id="freeText18322258142131746528" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395684i/762112._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i> <b> "This is a game. Our game. One that I asked for, but with each day it feels more real. More real than anything every has.... What to do. I shouldn't fall for this guy." </b></i> <br><br>When Cheyenne's heart is broken after finding her boyfriend in bed with another girl, she wants to find a way to make it clear to him that she doesn't need him in her life. Colt is struggling with pushing himself though school to keep a promise he made to his dying mother. When Cheyenne sees him in a coffee shop, she proposes a deal. She will pay him to pose as her boyfriend in an effort to make her ex jealous. Desperate for the money, he agrees and so begins their charade. Their game face they show the outside world. But the more the continue it, what feels most right in their lives is the charade.<br><br><b> <i> “This isn’t a fucking game anymore. No charades here. I don’t know exactly what to call it, but whatever it is, it’s ours. I’m going to latch onto it. And never let go.” </i> </b><br><br>The second half of this book was sooo good! It was heart breaking and had me in tears by about 90% (don't worry, there is still a HEA!). I did liked the story in the beginning and there were a few moment I really felt for but, overall I was a little distanced from the characters for the first half. No specific complaints. I liked each of them, I liked the story, I just wasn't feeling fully connected to it from the start, but I got steadily into it the more I read and about half way through, it got gooooood and my heart strings were pulled to the point of ending up in tears by the end. Ohhhh gosh, seriously, the 90% mark was painful!! My heart went right out to them.<br><br>I really liked the idea of how two people who barely even liked each other at first, who jumped to all the wrong conclusions about each other and seemingly weren't suited to each other at all ended up falling head over heals in love.<br><br><i> "Tomorrow... don't remind me I said this. I won't want to talk about it, but tonight... keep me safe." </i><br><br>We get alternating POVs that help familiarize us with how different each of their lives were and the pain they were each going through. I loved Colt's POV. What a sweet heart bad boy! He was really easy to fall for :)<br><br><i> <b> "No more games, I want you." he says into my ear." </b></i> <br><br>This book dealt with a lot of hard themes - young characters dealing with abandonment and death and trying to hold it together and stay strong. I loved that they were able to find support and strength in each other and that out of all the heart ache, they came away with each other and with a love and a bond that you knew was going to last.<br><br><i> "It's that stupid girl heart-pounding, hearts-floating-by-my-head thing. Where the guy who fights so hard to keep the distance, does something so small, it's huge. I can't help but let it inside. Let it mean something." </i><br><br>Its not very long and could be easily read in one sitting. If you are looking for an emotional New Adult read, its definitely one to consider!<br><br>Book 2 "<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16150320.Facade__The_Games_Series___2_" title="Facade (The Games Series, #2) by Nyrae Dawn" rel="nofollow noopener">Facade</a>" will follow the story of Colt's best friend Adrian (who we see a fair bit of in this book). I'm very much looking forward to his book which will be out Spring 2013.<br><br><b> CASTING: </b> I'm kind of seeing this guy as Colt... just tattoo him up in your minds and maybe dye his hair a little :P<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395684i/762113._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="18322258142131746528" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/452477852" />
    <a title="Kristen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5477946-kristen"><img alt="Kristen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1312922334p2/5477946.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/452477852?book_show_action=true">Nov 09, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristen" href="/user/show/5477946-kristen">Kristen</a>
      </span>

          marked it as did-not-finish


          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/16104077-charade">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=new-adult-college">new-adult-college</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=tattooed-pierced-hero">tattooed-pierced-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=book-everyone-loved-but-me">book-everyone-loved-but-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=needs-editing">needs-editing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=writing-style-didnt-work-for-me">writing-style-didnt-work-for-me</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer452477852" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15656603447107224950"><b>DNF at 48%</b><br/><br/>It kills me to mark this book DNF, as I know Nyrae Dawn is a much loved author with many of my friends <b>(sorry <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/3024056-karla' rel='nofollow noopener'> Karla</a>)</b>, but I don't think her writing style works for me. I had a devil of a time with the prose. I found it erratic and disjointed and in need of an editor to help with the pacing and transitions. For instance, flashback memories were confusing when they were interjected into current dialogue without the author indicating that such memories were taking place. It would have be</span>
  <span id="freeText15656603447107224950" style="display:none"><b>DNF at 48%</b><br /><br />It kills me to mark this book DNF, as I know Nyrae Dawn is a much loved author with many of my friends <b>(sorry <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/3024056-karla" rel="nofollow noopener"> Karla</a>)</b>, but I don't think her writing style works for me. I had a devil of a time with the prose. I found it erratic and disjointed and in need of an editor to help with the pacing and transitions. For instance, flashback memories were confusing when they were interjected into current dialogue without the author indicating that such memories were taking place. It would have been helpful had italics been used instead of quotation marks. The prose would not have felt so jarring. <br /><br />From what I read, I did LOVE the hero, Colt. He's everything I love in a bad boy who has a hidden golden heart. As for the heroine, Cheyenne, I really liked her at time, but her immaturity, melodrama, and random thoughts grated on my nerves. She was very young so I did take that into consideration. <br /><br />As much as I tried...and I really did try...I just wasn't able to get past the flow of the prose. That said, I cared enough about these characters to skip to the end to make sure they found their HEA. <br /><br /><br /></span>

          </span>

<div id="review_427572270" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Kellie Maddox-Ward" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7309666-kellie-maddox-ward"><img alt="Kellie Maddox-Ward" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1366371073p2/7309666.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/427572270?book_show_action=true">Oct 04, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kellie Maddox-Ward" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kellie Maddox-Ward" href="/user/show/7309666-kellie-maddox-ward">Kellie Maddox-Ward</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7309666-kellie-maddox-ward?shelf=college-romance">college-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer427572270" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3416911322595936039"><b>”I might not be able to do much for you, but I’ll hold your secrets.” – Colt </b><br/><br/>wow.<br/>WoW.<br/><b>WOW.</b><br/><i>
  <b>WOW.</b>
</i> <br/><br/>Anyone who knows me, knows I loved Nyrae’s writing and am totally a fangirl <br/><br/><a href='http://s1150.photobucket.com/albums/o606/lil_kel4/?action=view&current=fangirl.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393275i/757132.jpg' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I have read pretty much everything she has written in YA. This NA novel was awesome! <br/><br/>This book starts out with a bang! <i>(Yes bad Pun intended)</i> as Cheyenne walks in on her boyfriend of 2 years having sex with someone else in his College Dorm. <br/><br/>Chey has abandonment issues because of her Mom. She has so many walls up around h</span>
  <span id="freeText3416911322595936039" style="display:none"><b>”I might not be able to do much for you, but I’ll hold your secrets.” – Colt </b><br><br>wow.<br>WoW.<br><b>WOW.</b><br><i>
  <b>WOW.</b>
</i> <br><br>Anyone who knows me, knows I loved Nyrae’s writing and am totally a fangirl <br><br><a href="http://s1150.photobucket.com/albums/o606/lil_kel4/?action=view&amp;current=fangirl.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393275i/757132.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I have read pretty much everything she has written in YA. This NA novel was awesome! <br><br>This book starts out with a bang! <i>(Yes bad Pun intended)</i> as Cheyenne walks in on her boyfriend of 2 years having sex with someone else in his College Dorm. <br><br>Chey has abandonment issues because of her Mom. She has so many walls up around her that no-one can break through. She doesn’t actually love Greg, never did. But the fact he left her for someone else hurts. She decides that she can’t show him how much he hurt her.<br><br>Enter Colt.<br> <br>After seeing an altercation at the coffee shop between Greg and “Hot Tattoo Guy” she decides that she is going to approach Tattoo guy and see if he wants to play the game of Charades in front of Greg. <br><br>Colt turns her down. He is a badass tattoo guy who is basically an asshole and doesn’t have time to deal with the “Princess.” He has other things to worry about. His mother is dying of cancer, and to give her everything she has ever wanted to make her happy in the time she has left, Colt has taken up the role of a drug dealer.<br> <br>At a party Colt see’s Greg kiss Chey, when they are caught by Greg’s GF it becomes a bit of a scene. Colt can’t stand Greg so decides to walk up to Chey and accept the offer of the Charade. <br><br>What starts as a Charade for the rest of the world to see becomes real to Chey and Colt. They have never been themselves with anyone. Yet all of a sudden they are with each other. It was supposed to be having sex and hanging out for a distraction from their shitty lives. However it turns much more real than that as they begin to lean on each other for support, and the charade starts to crumble. <br><br><b>
  <i>In this half-dark room while my mother sleeps on the bed next to us, we make our vows to each other, to stop pretending. To grow up. To do what the hell we need to do to not be the people who had to play a fucked up game of charades to fall in love.</i>
</b><br><br><br>I love the cover of this book! I need to state that, it was real and suited the book. <br>However as soon as I started to read about Colt for some reason I pictured Chace Crawford<br><br><a href="http://s1150.photobucket.com/albums/o606/lil_kel4/?action=view&amp;current=colt3-1.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393275i/757133.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br> (with tattoo’s) and only confirmed it with this quote <br><br><i>
  <b>“But when he smiles? Really smiles, it’s perfect. Like toothpaste commercial, boy-next-door beauty that makes it really hard to be pissed at him.”</b>
</i><br><br><a href="http://s1150.photobucket.com/albums/o606/lil_kel4/?action=view&amp;current=colt2-1.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393275i/757134.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>There are still some funny giggle moments but it is very serious and <b>VERY</b> emotional as well. <br><br>In typical form it was written in both Chey and Colts POV that changed chapter to chapter so no confusion as whose POV you were reading from.<br>at about 84% my eyes were welling up for the rest of the book. <br><br>The sex scenes were fade to black. I can deal with that. Would of liked a bit more steam but that’s just me I’m a pervert. Oh and glad to see safe sex was being practiced! <br><br>I really liked the Epilogue it made me smile.<br> I also added to the end in my mind that they got married, become rich, got 2 dogs had a billion children so that they would never be alone anymore! <br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="3416911322595936039" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/409240865?book_show_action=true">Sep 07, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♥Rachel♥" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel">♥Rachel♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer409240865" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11809695531168577762">4.5 Stars<br/><br/><b>Charade</b> was not on my radar, but when I saw a ton of my Goodreads friends reading and loving it, I had to find out what all the commotion was about. I’m so glad I decided to pick this up, because it was such a beautiful and emotional story! This book made me cry, but I loved it anyhow! <br/><br/>Nineteen year-old Cheyenne, has just found out her boyfriend of two years, Gregory, is cheating on her. She followed him to college and thought they’d be together forever. To save face, Cheyenne falsely l</span>
  <span id="freeText11809695531168577762" style="display:none">4.5 Stars<br /><br /><b>Charade</b> was not on my radar, but when I saw a ton of my Goodreads friends reading and loving it, I had to find out what all the commotion was about. I’m so glad I decided to pick this up, because it was such a beautiful and emotional story! This book made me cry, but I loved it anyhow! <br /><br />Nineteen year-old Cheyenne, has just found out her boyfriend of two years, Gregory, is cheating on her. She followed him to college and thought they’d be together forever. To save face, Cheyenne falsely led Gregory to believe that someone else was interested in her, and now with him out of the way, she was going to go for it. When she runs into Colt, and sees the animosity between Gregory and him, she approaches him to make a deal. Pretend to be her boyfriend she’ll pay. Cheyenne has created a careful façade of being strong and happy, and she needs to keep it up. She doesn’t want people know she’s hurt or affected by Gregory, to see weakness in her.<br /><br />Colt is a typical bad-boy, on the surface. He’s strikingly handsome, but with tattoos and attitude for days, he has an edge to him. Underneath, he’s struggling to keep things together. His mother is dying of cancer and with her being a single parent, there’s no father to shoulder the weight or responsibility of her care. He loves his mother. She always put his well being first and is the reason he worked hard to get into college. When Cheyenne first proposes her deal, he shrugs her off as a shallow princess only caring about what others think of her. <br /><br />Cheyenne has worked hard at keeping people at arm’s length, dealing with abandonment issues from her mother leaving her at a young age. Her thinking is if you don’t let them too close, they won’t have the power to hurt you. At first, because she doesn’t really care what Colt thinks of her, she allows him to see her true self. I think she realized Colt was someone who could understand her darkness, and wouldn’t judge her for it. Cheyenne is completely opposite of the spoiled princess Colt thought she was at first. He finds a kindred spirit in her and before you know it, these two have a connection neither was planning on. I just loved these two broken souls trying to deal with their pasts and being there for each other. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>”I thought this was a game,” I remind him. “Not anymore and you know it. Everything else in my life is all f%*ked up. This is the only thing that’s real.” I gasp. It’s what I want to hear. What I need to hear. What I feel in each of my scarred heartbeats. </i>
</b> <br /><br />Like I said in the outset, this story made me cry. I lost my Mom when I was twenty-one and went through much of the same experience as Colt, so it was easy to feel his pain. His relationship with his mom was so heartbreaking. They didn’t have the best circumstances, but love was the predominant quality between them. I think that’s why he had so much to give to Cheyenne. <br /><br />Ms. Dawn’s writing found a way into my heart, it was poignant and felt real. This certainly won’t be the last story I pick up from her. I’m officially a fan! <br /><br />Favorite quote: <br /><br /><b>
  <i>“This isn't a f&amp;*king game anymore. No charades here. I don't know exactly what to call it, but whatever it is, it's ours. I'm going to latch onto it. And never let it go.”</i>
</b>--Colt<br /><br />You can find this review and more at <a href="http://thereadersden.blogspot.com/2012/11/review-charade-by-nyrae-dawn.html" rel="nofollow noopener">The Readers Den.</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="11809695531168577762" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_453520113" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/453520113" />
    <a title="♡Karlyn P♡" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1131400-karlyn-p"><img alt="♡Karlyn P♡" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1389996373p2/1131400.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/453520113?book_show_action=true">Nov 11, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♡Karlyn P♡" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♡Karlyn P♡" href="/user/show/1131400-karlyn-p">♡Karlyn P♡</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1131400-karlyn-p?shelf=steam-warm">steam-warm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1131400-karlyn-p?shelf=genre-youngadult">genre-youngadult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer453520113" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10486849491249490732"><br/><b>3.5* 'Where are the last names, folks?!' stars.</b><br/><br/>Summary: I liked it, but no "OMG!" gushing here folks. <br/><br/>Charade is a quick YA-M read with some emotional twists that will guarantee to make you cry at the end, but the romance and relationship was pretty standard fare. Fans of angst-filled college life stories with some steamy parts, some family life drama, and a budding romance between two opposite types will enjoy this one. <br/><br/>There was an odd generic simplicity with the story, which didn't bother me </span>
  <span id="freeText10486849491249490732" style="display:none"><br /><b>3.5* 'Where are the last names, folks?!' stars.</b><br /><br />Summary: I liked it, but no "OMG!" gushing here folks. <br /><br />Charade is a quick YA-M read with some emotional twists that will guarantee to make you cry at the end, but the romance and relationship was pretty standard fare. Fans of angst-filled college life stories with some steamy parts, some family life drama, and a budding romance between two opposite types will enjoy this one. <br /><br />There was an odd generic simplicity with the story, which didn't bother me too much but it did leave me wanting to know more about these people and their lives. <b>Nothing seemed to have full names and identities. None of the characters had last names, the college name was unspecified, the town and state was unspecified and could be Anywhere, USA. Even Colt's mothers cancer type was unspecified. She just had cancer. The coffee shop was just that - the coffee shop. And so forth. </b><br /><br />Cheyenne catches her boyfriend of two-years, Greg, in bed with another girl, Red, which triggers her to lie about having another guy interested in her. Colt, a tattooed college junior, and Greg are fast enemies. When Cheyenne witnesses a confrontation between these two, she approaches him with a game plan of Charades. This is meant to sooth her ego more than it is to make Greg jealous. Colt refuses at first, but later agrees. Cheyenne and Colt start off on a rocky path and many small fights occur, but in no time the game of Charades fades away and it becomes something real. <br /><br />Despite the generic tone of the story, it did have a surprising amount of depth (but I would have liked more!) We might not learn their last names or even what town they live in, but we learn enough about their personal lives to believe in these two. Their family lives are center to the story, and it will absolutely tug at your heart. <br /><br />The romance moved pretty fast, despite being fresh out of a two year relationship. The ex-boyfriend Greg was a bit of an anomaly. He didn't have much of a role except to incite problems every few chapters. Colt was probably the best part of this story, I think we learn the most about him and see him go through the most emotional angst. The bad-boy who doesn't want to get serious finds his match with Cheyenne. <br /><br />I did enjoy this one, but wasn't blown away. The romance took time to warm up and make me believe that these two really cared for each other, but by the end I was convinced. There is a secondary story between Colt and his mother which was quite tender, and IMO it out shined the main romance story between him and Cheyenne. <br /><br /><br /> </span>
  <a data-text-id="10486849491249490732" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_451657636" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/451657636" />
    <a title="AJ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3143126-aj"><img alt="AJ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406382884p2/3143126.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/451657636?book_show_action=true">Nov 08, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AJ" href="/user/show/3143126-aj">AJ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=drama">drama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series-standalone">series-standalone</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=feeeeels">feeeeels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series-book-1">series-book-1</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=pb-i-own">pb-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=sob-fest">sob-fest</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=omg-romantic">omg-romantic</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer451657636" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8097798539598439377"><b>WOW! JUST…. WOW. <u>SUCH</u> A BEAUTIFUL BOOK!!!</b><br/><br/>I’m such a sucker for the fake relationship set up, so this was a winner for me before I even started. But it soon became clear to me that there is so much more to this book. The way they initially came together is a little weird, but is an indicator of how screwed up these two characters are at the beginning of the story, and a great starting point for some major character development. <br/><br/>Colt and Cheyenne are two very real, very honest (and yes, screwed up</span>
  <span id="freeText8097798539598439377" style="display:none"><b>WOW! JUST…. WOW. <u>SUCH</u> A BEAUTIFUL BOOK!!!</b><br /><br />I’m such a sucker for the fake relationship set up, so this was a winner for me before I even started. But it soon became clear to me that there is so much more to this book. The way they initially came together is a little weird, but is an indicator of how screwed up these two characters are at the beginning of the story, and a great starting point for some major character development. <br /><br />Colt and Cheyenne are two very real, very honest (and yes, screwed up) characters. Cheyenne has some trauma in her past, while Colt is dealing with some major stuff in his present. With their fake relationship fizzling out but developing into a tentative friendship, both of them are looking for a way to deal with their pain, and they turn to each other, finding a way to be together in a way that helps them forget about all of the drama in their lives. But this quickly develops into more as two people who never let anybody close, discover that they actually make each other’s lives better. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>I grab her arms and pull her toward me. Now she has her arms wrapped around my waist and we’re chest to chest. She’s laughing and I almost want to laugh with her. For a second it feels real and okay. The knot in my gut loosens and I’m not scared to breathe. </i>
</b><br /><br />Amidst the funny banter, and some gorgeously tender moments, the romance develops slowly and realistically. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>“I thought this was a game,” I remind him. <br />“Not anymore and you know it. Everything else in my life is all fucked up. This is the only thing that’s real.” </i>
</b><br /><br />And watching them both realise that they’d finally let somebody in and fallen for each other was just magic. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>I don’t know how in the fuck we got here, but somehow this game is more real than anything else.<br />And I want it.<br />I fucking want it.</i>
</b><br /><br />I fell in instant love with both Colt and Chey. The interactions and dialogue between them is incredibly real and with the story being in both of their POVs, we get right inside of their heads to see what they are going through, and it’s sensational. I could very easily put myself in their positions and understand everything that they were feeling. They were both honest with each other, and there was no stupidness at all. And not once did I want to smack either of them (believe me - this is a rare event that should be treasured!).<br /><br /><b>
  <i>This isn’t a fucking game anymore. No charades here. I don’t know exactly what to call it, but whatever it is, it’s ours. I’m going to latch onto it. And never let go. </i>
</b><br /><br />This is a beautifully written, very emotional read. The things that the characters go through are intense and heartbreakingly tragic (I was in tears for an entire chapter!). But there is enough humour, lightness and swoony romance to balance out the heavier stuff nicely. The highlight of the book for me was watching them go through everything they went through together, leaning on each other, but still standing strong, it was just beautiful. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>We may have been brought together because of a stupid ass game. Or because we were both screwed up, or needed to change, but we got somewhere important and that’s the only thing that counts. </i>
</b><br /><br />I absolutely loved this story, and read it in one sitting, unable to put it down. It was my first book from Nyrae Dawn, and I can’t wait to read more from this incredibly talented author. <br /><br />4.5 stars!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8097798539598439377" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1654917759" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1654917759" />
    <a title="Irene Sim" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31914348-irene-sim"><img alt="Irene Sim" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1565617599p2/31914348.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1654917759?book_show_action=true">Sep 12, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Irene Sim" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Irene Sim" href="/user/show/31914348-irene-sim">Irene Sim</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31914348-irene-sim?shelf=2016-read">2016-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31914348-irene-sim?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31914348-irene-sim?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31914348-irene-sim?shelf=contemporary-fiction">contemporary-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31914348-irene-sim?shelf=2018-read">2018-read</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1654917759" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer263581974212318755">I'm adding half a star with my 2018 reread of this story. The rest of my previous review stands as it is but I guess I appreciated the author's work more this second time. It was a delight to revisit Colt and Chey's story, they are two unique characters and I really loved them. I'm curious about Adrian's story and I think it's about time to start his book....<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1543215923i/26649020._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>3,5 stars! <br/>I really liked this story. It was very emotional with many heart-warming and heart-wrenching scenes without being cheesy or lame</span>
  <span id="freeText263581974212318755" style="display:none">I'm adding half a star with my 2018 reread of this story. The rest of my previous review stands as it is but I guess I appreciated the author's work more this second time. It was a delight to revisit Colt and Chey's story, they are two unique characters and I really loved them. I'm curious about Adrian's story and I think it's about time to start his book....<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1543215923i/26649020._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>3,5 stars! <br>I really liked this story. It was very emotional with many heart-warming and heart-wrenching scenes without being cheesy or lame about it. <br>The main characters are Cheyenne, a nineteen y.o. girl who struggles to come to terms with her mother's abandonment in early childhood, and twenty-one y.o. Colton "Colt" who is losing his only parent to a fatal disease. <br>In the middle of the whirlwind that's their everyday life, these two lost souls find in each other the calm and peace that's been absent for so long. It is a beautiful story indeed. <br>Then why only 3,5 stars you'll wonder. Though it is a beautiful story, as I aforementioned, it isn't beautifully told. <s>Many spelling or grammar errors bordering to annoying and many second characters unexplored.</s> <br>Also, I had a major issue with the cover. Seeing this cover what first comes to mind is that the story is another romantic comedy, a fun and light read. You couldn't be more wrong. I often don't pay much attention to the covers, there are so many shirtless guys out there so what's one more, but in this case I felt that it devalued the depth of the story. Their relationship wasn't as light or as easy as the cover insinuates.<br>Anyway, that's just my opinion, and I'm definitely going to read more of the author's works.</span>
  <a data-text-id="263581974212318755" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer449036468" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer14952787889676723171"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390504175i/8233651._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396591i/764652._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Fantastic. I really enjoyed this book. I've given it four stars because I felt that it was a bit predictable, but other than that, it was great.<br/><br/>The situation with Colt's Mum was so heart breaking, yet so beautiful. I loved the person Colt became when he was with her and I enjoyed reading his POV, even though it was devastatingly sad. This is a real tear jerker.<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>"He loves you," she adds. "And I love you. You're everything I could have hoped for, for him."</i>
</blockquote><br/><br/>I loved how each of the characters drew</span>
  <span id="freeText14952787889676723171" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390504175i/8233651._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396591i/764652._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Fantastic. I really enjoyed this book. I've given it four stars because I felt that it was a bit predictable, but other than that, it was great.<br><br>The situation with Colt's Mum was so heart breaking, yet so beautiful. I loved the person Colt became when he was with her and I enjoyed reading his POV, even though it was devastatingly sad. This is a real tear jerker.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"He loves you," she adds. "And I love you. You're everything I could have hoped for, for him."</i>
</blockquote><br><br>I loved how each of the characters drew strength from one another and each endured their own hardships, whilst steadfastly supporting the other. Their relationship was so beautiful and so unexpected for both of them.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"I thought this was a game," I reminded him.<br>"Not anymore and you know it. Everything else in my life is all f*cked up. This is the only thing that's real." </i>
</blockquote><br><br>There was a lot of pain in this book, but it made the moments of joy and love all the more intense. <br><br>Aside from all of the hurt, anguish and also romance... Colt is hot. It's got to be said. People may die and there may be a lot of heartbreak, but credit where credit is due, Colt will get your panties in a twist!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"I'm fucking good at this boyfriend shit. Who would have thought?"</i>
</blockquote><br><br>I really enjoyed Nyrae Dawn's writing style and I do love a good alternate POV book. I'll definitely be investigating more of her work in the future.<br><br>To read more reviews go to my Book Blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/">http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/</a><br>Follow me on Twitter: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://twitter.com/SmittenSC">https://twitter.com/SmittenSC</a><br>Find me on Pinterest: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://pinterest.com/smittensc/">http://pinterest.com/smittensc/</a></span>

<div id="review_451613522" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/451613522" />
    <a title="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog"><img alt="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1416791332p2/4597644.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/451613522?book_show_action=true">Nov 08, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" href="/user/show/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog">Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=highly-emotional">highly-emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=lead-character-bad-boy">lead-character-bad-boy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=hot-and-heavy">hot-and-heavy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=lead-character-player">lead-character-player</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=new-adult-mature-ya">new-adult-mature-ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=must-re-read-again">must-re-read-again</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=lead-character-tattooed-and-sexy">lead-character-tattooed-and-sexy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=ultimate-book-boyfriend">ultimate-book-boyfriend</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=crack-books">crack-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer451613522" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8741976630301790713">Five Stars<br/><br/><b>
  <i>That’s what we have – we’re both damaged with baggage and somehow it works.</i>
</b><br/><br/>**Wipes away tears** I’m crying like a baby, but I don’t care. <b>I ABSOLUTELY LOVED THIS!</b> **Sniff** Wow! This was a pleasant surprise. After my last read, which was angst on steroids, I wanted something light and predictable. This my friends, was not light, though it was a little predictable. The H/h were both incredible characters and their story is chalk full of emotions, anger and love. It all equaled to on</span>
  <span id="freeText8741976630301790713" style="display:none">Five Stars<br /><br /><b>
  <i>That’s what we have – we’re both damaged with baggage and somehow it works.</i>
</b><br /><br />**Wipes away tears** I’m crying like a baby, but I don’t care. <b>I ABSOLUTELY LOVED THIS!</b> **Sniff** Wow! This was a pleasant surprise. After my last read, which was angst on steroids, I wanted something light and predictable. This my friends, was not light, though it was a little predictable. The H/h were both incredible characters and their story is chalk full of emotions, anger and love. It all equaled to one big beautiful story. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>He has dark blond, clouds-over-sunset colored hair. It’s messy, like he hasn’t combed it all day. A black t-shirt stretches across his chest and all the way down his right arm are tattoos. Like, so many of them I can’t even see his skin.</i>
</b><br /><br />Tattoos. With that one word describing our Hero, Colt, I immediately fell in love. Superficial of me, I know, but I can’t help what I like and fantasize about. However underneath his tough guy exterior, lays a man who is going through the toughest time of his life. His beloved mother is dying. She is all the family he has left and means the world to him. He’s a good son, most of the time. All his mother wants is for Colt to be happy. She constantly encourages him to be a better man. No more drug dealing and concentrate on school. Colt tries, but his overwhelming feeling of responsibility to help his mom, financially and emotionally, take a toll on him. Where else can he make fast money to help?<br /><br /><b>
  <i>This is a game. Our game. One that I asked for, but with each day it feels more real.</i>
</b><br /><br />Cheyenne is prone to panic attacks. When she was very young, her mother abandoned her during a party. There’s more to that story as we later find out, but just know, it does a number on her. She refuses to let anyone too close to her. Even her sleazy, now ex-boyfriend never got that close. But still. She had plans with Gregory. He was her normal, but the bastard broke her heart anyway. <br /><br /><b>
  <i> I vow to myself right then and there I will never make that mistake again. People hurt you if you let them. I won’t be hurt again. </i>
</b><br /><br />After being together for two years, she caught Gregory cheating on her. Not only that, but apparently the jackass accidentally let it slip that it was more than a one time thing. Dumbass. He does his best to convince her its still she he loves, but she’s buying any of that bull. So she dumps him. Before they part ways, she’s casually mentions that he wasn’t the only guy interested in her. Unfortunately, all her friends are all his friends. She needed to prove to him, to them all, that she can move beyond this. After seeing Colt and Gregory argue, she decides then and there exactly how to punish and piss off Gregory. An arrangement is made that changes both, Cheyenne and Colt's lives. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>Something happens inside my chest. I’ve been really good at keeping him at arm’s length so far. We’re nothing alike. I think he hates me half the time and we don’t belong together. We’re a means to an end, but with his simple request, I begin to soften inside…<br />I should leave. Run right now because Colt and I wouldn’t work.</i>
</b><br /><br />These two clashed from the very beginning. They got on each other’s nerves and fought…a lot. However, for some strange odd reason, they find solace and comfort with each other. They were both reluctant at first, but fate keeps intervening and they find themselves constantly being thrown together. <br /><br />Cheyenne never thought she would open up to anyone, ever, but when she needs someone, Colt is always there, comforting her. Colt is having a tough time with his ailing mother, but found himself happy when he’s with Cheyenne. No girl has ever made him feel wanted or needed like she did. Together they made sense and together they begin to heal. <br /><br />Fuck. I LOVED this story. I just fell in love with everything that happened. There were several times I swooned and a couple of times I just outright cried. Such a moving and beautiful story. This is my first Nyrae Dawn book and it will most definitely not be my last. I HIGHLY RECOMMEND!!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8741976630301790713" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_409780475" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/409780475" />
    <a title="Jenn" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3349239-jenn"><img alt="Jenn" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1397155775p2/3349239.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/409780475?book_show_action=true">Sep 07, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jenn" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jenn" href="/user/show/3349239-jenn">Jenn</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">anyone who LOVES this author</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Jenn by: </span>
       buddy read: Jojo, Lindsay &amp; Bethany
